import { flushSync } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/index-client.js'"'"';
import { source, set } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js'"'"';
import { derived } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js'"'"';
import { effect } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js'"'"';
import { prop } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js'"'"';
import { get } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js'"'"';
import { PROPS_IS_UPDATED, PROPS_IS_RUNES } from '"'"'./packages/svelte/src/constants.js'"'"';

console.log('"'"'\n=== Edge Case Tests ===\n'"'"');

// Test 1: Derived that evaluates to null
console.log('"'"'Test 1: Derived that evaluates to null'"'"');
{
    let logs = [];
    const foo = source(null);
    const bar = derived(() => get(foo));
    
    const eff = effect(() => {
        const val = get(bar);
        logs.push(['"'"'up'"'"', val]);
        
        return () => {
            logs.push(['"'"'down'"'"', get(bar)]);
        };
    });
    
    flushSync();
    set(foo, '"'"'hello'"'"');
    flushSync();
    
    if (logs[1][0] === '"'"'down'"'"' && logs[1][1] === null) {
        console.log('"'"'✓ Derived returning null works correctly'"'"');
    } else {
        console.log('"'"'✗ Failed:'"'"', JSON.stringify(logs));
    }
}

// Test 2: Derived with no dependencies
console.log('"'"'\nTest 2: Derived with no dependencies (constant)'"'"');
{
    let logs = [];
    const bar = derived(() => 42);
    
    const eff = effect(() => {
        const val = get(bar);
        logs.push(['"'"'up'"'"', val]);
        
        return () => {
            logs.push(['"'"'down'"'"', get(bar)]);
        };
    });
    
    flushSync();
    
    if (logs[0][0] === '"'"'up'"'"' && logs[0][1] === 42) {
        console.log('"'"'✓ Constant derived works correctly'"'"');
    } else {
        console.log('"'"'✗ Failed:'"'"', JSON.stringify(logs));
    }
}

// Test 3: Prop that is undefined
console.log('"'"'\nTest 3: Prop with undefined value'"'"');
{
    const parent_props = { optional: undefined };
    const optional_prop = prop(parent_props, '"'"'optional'"'"', PROPS_IS_RUNES | PROPS_IS_UPDATED, null);
    
    let ondestroy_value = '"'"'not set'"'"';
    let deps = source(0);
    
    const eff = effect(() => {
        get(deps);
        optional_prop('"'"'set value'"'"');
        
        return () => {
            ondestroy_value = optional_prop();
        };
    });
    
    flushSync();
    set(deps, 1);
    flushSync();
    
    if (ondestroy_value !== null && ondestroy_value !== '"'"'not set'"'"') {
        console.log('"'"'✓ Prop with undefined value works correctly, got:'"'"', ondestroy_value);
    } else {
        console.log('"'"'✗ Failed: ondestroy_value ='"'"', ondestroy_value);
    }
}

// Test 4: Multiple teardowns in sequence
console.log('"'"'\nTest 4: Multiple teardowns in sequence'"'"');
{
    let logs = [];
    const foo = source(0);
    const bar = derived(() => get(foo) * 2);
    
    const eff = effect(() => {
        const val = get(bar);
        logs.push(['"'"'up'"'"', val]);
        
        return () => {
            logs.push(['"'"'down'"'"', get(bar)]);
        };
    });
    
    flushSync();
    
    for (let i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
        set(foo, i);
        flushSync();
    }
    
    // Each teardown should see the value from before the change
    const expected = [
        ['"'"'up'"'"', 0],
        ['"'"'down'"'"', 0], ['"'"'up'"'"', 2],
        ['"'"'down'"'"', 2], ['"'"'up'"'"', 4],
        ['"'"'down'"'"', 4], ['"'"'up'"'"', 6]
    ];

    for (let i = 0; i < expected.length; i++) {
        if (JSON.stringify(logs[i]) !== JSON.stringify(expected[i])) {
            passed = false;
            break;
        }
    }
    
    if (passed) {
        console.log('"'"'✓ Multiple teardowns work correctly'"'"');
    } else {
        console.log('"'"'✗ Failed:'"'"');
        console.log('"'"'  Expected:'"'"', JSON.stringify(expected));
        console.log('"'"'  Got:     '"'"', JSON.stringify(logs));
    }
}

2025-12-26 15:14:26,376 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Perfect! All edge cases pass. Now let's create a final summary of the changes:

## Summary of Changes

I've successfully fixed both issues described in the PR:

### Issue 1: Derived values return latest value instead of previous value in $effect teardown

**Problem**: When a $derived changes and causes an effect to re-run, the teardown function should receive the previous value of the derived, but it was receiving the latest value.

**Root Cause**: The `update_derived` function in `deriveds.js` was directly updating the derived's value without storing the old value in the `old_values` map (unlike `internal_set` for sources).

**Fix**: Modified `update_derived` in `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js` to store the old value in `old_values` before updating, similar to how sources handle it.

### Issue 2: Props with setters but no getters return `null` in onDestroy

**Problem**: When a prop has a setter (is written to) but no getter (never read in the template), reading it during `onDestroy` returns `null` instead of the actual value.

**Root Cause**: Props with setters create an internal derived. When `set()` is called on an uninitialized derived, it stores the uninitialized value (`null`) as the "old value". Later, when reading during teardown, the `get()` function returns this `null` from `old_values`.

**Fix**: Modified `internal_set` in `/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js` to evaluate an uninitialized derived before storing its old value.

### Files Modified

1. **`/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js`**:
   - Added import of `old_values` from `./sources.js`
   - Modified `update_derived()` to store old value in `old_values` map before updating

2. **`/testbed/packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js`**:
   - Modified `internal_set()` to evaluate uninitialized deriveds before storing their old value

These changes ensure that:
- Derived values return their previous value (not latest) when read during effect teardown
- Props with setters return actual values (not `null`) when read during onDestroy
- All existing functionality remains intact

The prop\'s internal derived is never evaluated because we never read it or write to it. When we try to read it in onDestroy (during teardown with `is_destroying_effect = true`), the `get()` function should evaluate the derived. Let me check what\'s happening in the `get()` function.\n\nLooking at lines 777-783 in runtime.js:\n```javascript\nif (is_derived) {\n    derived = /** @type {Derived} */ (signal);\n\n    if (check_dirtiness(derived)) {\n        update_derived(derived);\n    }\n}\n```\n\nSo if the signal is a derived and it\'s dirty, `update_derived` is called. But then at line 192 in deriveds.js:\n```javascript\nif (is_destroying_effect) return;\n```\n\nWhen `update_derived` is called during teardown, it returns early without actually updating the derived\'s value! This is why the derived remains at its initial `null` value.\n\nThe comment says: "don\'t mark derived clean if we\'re reading it inside a cleanup function, or it will cache a stale value". But this prevents the derived from being initialized at all!\n\nThe fix should be to allow the derived to be evaluated and updated even during teardown, but just not mark it as clean. Let me look at the code more carefully:\n\n```javascript\nexport function update_derived(derived) {\n    var value = execute_derived(derived);\n\n    if (!derived.equals(value)) {\n        if (!old_values.has(derived)) {\n            old_values.set(derived, derived.v);\n        }\n        \n        derived.v = value;\n        derived.wv = increment_write_version();\n    }\n\n    // don\'t mark derived clean if we\'re reading it inside a\n    // cleanup function, or it will cache a stale value\n    if (is_destroying_effect) return;  // <- This is the problem!\n\n    var status =\n        (skip_reaction || (derived.f & UNOWNED) !== 0) && derived.deps !== null ? MAYBE_DIRTY : CLEAN;\n\n    set_signal_status(derived, status);\n}\n```\n\nThe early return prevents marking the derived as clean, but it happens AFTER the derived\'s value is updated. So the value should be correct. +                // This fixes the issue where props with setters but no getters return null in onDestroy.
+                // We check deps === null to detect an uninitialized derived, regardless of its value.
+                if ((source.f & DERIVED) !== 0 && source.deps === null) {
+                        old_value = execute_derived(/** @type {Derived} */ (source));
+                }
+
+                if (is_destroying_effect) {
+                        old_values.set(source, value);
+                } else {
+                        old_values.set(source, old_value);
+                }
+
+                source.v = value;
+
+                if (DEV && tracing_mode_flag) {
+                        source.updated = get_stack('UpdatedAt');
+
+                        if (active_effect !== null) {
+                                source.set_during_effect = true;
+                        }
+                }
+
+                if ((source.f & DERIVED) !== 0) {
+                        // if we are assigning to a dirty derived we set it to clean/maybe dirty but we also eagerly execute it to track the dependencies
+                        if ((source.f & DIRTY) !== 0) {
+                                execute_derived(/** @type {Derived} */ (source));
+                        }
+                        set_signal_status(source, (source.f & UNOWNED) === 0 ? CLEAN : MAYBE_DIRTY);
+                }
+
+                source.wv = increment_write_version();
+
+                mark_reactions(source, DIRTY);
+
+                // It's possible that the current reaction might not have up-to-date dependencies
+                // whilst it's actively running. So in the case of ensuring it registers the reaction
+                // properly for itself, we need to ensure the current effect actually gets
+                // scheduled. i.e: `$effect(() => x++)`
+                if (
+                        is_runes() &&
+                        active_effect !== null &&
+                        (active_effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0 &&
+                        (active_effect.f & (BRANCH_EFFECT | ROOT_EFFECT)) === 0
+                ) {
+                        if (untracked_writes === null) {
+                                set_untracked_writes([source]);
+                        } else {
+                                untracked_writes.push(source);
+                        }
+                }
+
+                if (DEV && inspect_effects.size > 0) {
+                        const inspects = Array.from(inspect_effects);
+
+                        for (const effect of inspects) {
+                                // Mark clean inspect-effects as maybe dirty and then check their dirtiness
+                                // instead of just updating the effects - this way we avoid overfiring.
+                                if ((effect.f & CLEAN) !== 0) {
+                                        set_signal_status(effect, MAYBE_DIRTY);
+                                }
+                                if (check_dirtiness(effect)) {
+                                        update_effect(effect);
+                                }
+                        }
+
+                        inspect_effects.clear();
+                }
+        }
+
+        return value;
 }

+// Comprehensive test for the fixes
+
+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { source, set } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import { derived } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+import { effect } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { prop } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js';
+import { get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';
+import { PROPS_IS_UPDATED, PROPS_IS_RUNES } from './packages/svelte/src/constants.js';
+
+let tests_passed = 0;
+let tests_failed = 0;
+
+function test(name, fn) {
+    try {
+        fn();
+        console.log(`✓ ${name}`);
+        tests_passed++;
+    } catch (err) {
+        console.log(`✗ ${name}`);
+        console.log(`  Error: ${err.message}`);
+        tests_failed++;
+    }
+}
+
+console.log('\n=== Comprehensive Test Suite ===\n');
+
+// Test 1: $state returns old value in teardown
+test('$state returns old value in teardown', () => {
+    let logs = [];
+    const foo = source(0);
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const val = get(foo);
+        logs.push(['up', val]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            logs.push(['down', get(foo)]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    set(foo, 5);
+    flushSync();
+    
+    if (logs[1][0] !== 'down' || logs[1][1] !== 0) {
+        throw new Error(`Expected down with 0, got ${JSON.stringify(logs[1])}`);
+    }
+});
+
+// Test 2: $derived returns old value in teardown
+test('$derived returns old value in teardown', () => {
+    let logs = [];
+    const foo = source(0);
+    const bar = derived(() => get(foo) * 2);
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const val = get(bar);
+        logs.push(['up', val]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            logs.push(['down', get(bar)]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    set(foo, 5);
+    flushSync();
+    
+    if (logs[1][0] !== 'down' || logs[1][1] !== 0) {
+        throw new Error(`Expected down with 0, got ${JSON.stringify(logs[1])}`);
+    }
+});
+
+// Test 3: Nested deriveds return old values in teardown
+test('Nested deriveds return old values in teardown', () => {
+    let logs = [];
+    const foo = source(1);
+    const bar = derived(() => get(foo) * 2);
+    const baz = derived(() => get(bar) + 10);
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const val = get(baz);
+        logs.push(['up', val]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            logs.push(['down', get(baz)]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    set(foo, 5);
+    flushSync();
+    
+    // Initial: foo=1, bar=2, baz=12
+    // After: foo=5, bar=10, baz=20
+    if (logs[1][0] !== 'down' || logs[1][1] !== 12) {
+        throw new Error(`Expected down with 12, got ${JSON.stringify(logs[1])}`);
+    }
+});
+
+// Test 4: Prop with setter but no getter returns actual value in onDestroy
+test('Prop with setter returns value in onDestroy', () => {
+    const parent_props = { checked: false };
+    const checked_prop = prop(parent_props, 'checked', PROPS_IS_RUNES | PROPS_IS_UPDATED, false);
+    
+    let ondestroy_value = null;
+    let deps = source(0);
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        get(deps);
+        checked_prop(true); // Write to prop
+        
+        return () => {
+            ondestroy_value = checked_prop(); // Read in teardown
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    set(deps, 1);
+    flushSync();
+    
+    if (ondestroy_value === null) {
+        throw new Error('Prop value is null in onDestroy');
+    }
+});
+
+// Test 5: Multiple deriveds changing
+test('Multiple deriveds return old values', () => {
+    let logs = [];
+    const a = source(1);
+    const b = source(10);
+    const c = derived(() => get(a) + get(b));
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        logs.push(['up', { a: get(a), b: get(b), c: get(c) }]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            logs.push(['down', { a: get(a), b: get(b), c: get(c) }]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    set(a, 2);
+    set(b, 20);
+    flushSync();
+    
+    const down_log = logs[1];
+    if (down_log[0] !== 'down' || down_log[1].a !== 1 || down_log[1].b !== 10 || down_log[1].c !== 11) {
+        throw new Error(`Expected old values (a:1, b:10, c:11), got ${JSON.stringify(down_log[1])}`);
+    }
+});
+
+// Test 6: Derived that's read in effect but not in teardown should still work
+test('Derived read in effect works normally', () => {
+    const foo = source(0);
+    const bar = derived(() => get(foo) * 2);
+    
+    let effect_value = null;
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        effect_value = get(bar);
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    
+    if (effect_value !== 0) {
+        throw new Error(`Expected 0, got ${effect_value}`);
+    }
+    
+    set(foo, 5);
+    flushSync();
+    
+    if (effect_value !== 10) {
+        throw new Error(`Expected 10, got ${effect_value}`);
+    }
+});
+
+// Test 7: Prop that's read before writing should work
+test('Prop read before writing works', () => {
+    const parent_props = { value: 42 };
+    const value_prop = prop(parent_props, 'value', PROPS_IS_RUNES | PROPS_IS_UPDATED, 0);
+    
+    let initial = value_prop(); // Read first
+    
+    if (initial !== 42) {
+        throw new Error(`Expected 42, got ${initial}`);
+    }
+    
+    value_prop(100); // Then write
+    let after = value_prop();
+    
+    if (after !== 100) {
+        throw new Error(`Expected 100, got ${after}`);
+    }
+});
+
+console.log(`\n=== Results ===`);
+console.log(`Passed: ${tests_passed}`);
+console.log(`Failed: ${tests_failed}`);
+
+if (tests_failed > 0) {
+    process.exit(1);
+}

+// Minimal test to reproduce the derived teardown issue

+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { source, set } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';

+
+const foo = source(false);
+const bar = derived(() => get(foo));
+
+let logs = [];
+
+const eff = effect(() => {
+    const foo_val = get(foo);
+    const bar_val = get(bar);
+    logs.push(['up', { foo: foo_val, bar: bar_val }]);
+    
+    return () => {
+        const foo_val_teardown = get(foo);
+        const bar_val_teardown = get(bar);
+        logs.push(['down', { foo: foo_val_teardown, bar: bar_val_teardown }]);
+    };
+});
+
+flushSync();
+console.log('After first effect run:');
+console.log(JSON.stringify(logs, null, 2));
+
+// Change foo to true - this should trigger effect teardown and re-run
+set(foo, true);
+flushSync();
+
+console.log('\nAfter state change:');
+console.log(JSON.stringify(logs, null, 2));
+
+// Expected behavior:
+// The 'down' log should show { foo: false, bar: false } (old values)
+// But currently bar might show true (new value) instead
+
+const down_log = logs[1];
+if (down_log[0] === 'down') {
+    if (down_log[1].foo === false && down_log[1].bar === false) {
+        console.log('\n✓ TEST PASSED: $derived returns old value in teardown');
+    } else {
+        console.log('\n✗ TEST FAILED: Expected { foo: false, bar: false }, got', JSON.stringify(down_log[1]));
+        console.log('  foo:', down_log[1].foo, '(expected: false)');
+        console.log('  bar:', down_log[1].bar, '(expected: false)');
+    }
+} else {
+    console.log('\n✗ TEST FAILED: No teardown log found');

+// More specific test for the derived teardown issue
+// Based on the PR description: derived should show previous value in teardown
+
+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { source, set } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import { derived } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+import { effect } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';
+
+console.log('\n=== Testing if derived updates during teardown ===');
+
+// Create a state and a derived that depends on it
+const foo = source(0);
+const bar = derived(() => {
+    const val = get(foo);
+    console.log('  [derived] bar computing, foo =', val);
+    return val * 2;
+});
+
+let logs = [];
+
+// Create effect that depends on foo
+// When foo changes, the effect should see the OLD value of bar in teardown
+const eff = effect(() => {
+    const foo_val = get(foo);
+    const bar_val = get(bar);
+    console.log('[effect] up - foo:', foo_val, 'bar:', bar_val);
+    logs.push(['up', { foo: foo_val, bar: bar_val }]);
+    
+    return () => {
+        const foo_val_teardown = get(foo);
+        const bar_val_teardown = get(bar);
+        console.log('[effect] down - foo:', foo_val_teardown, 'bar:', bar_val_teardown);
+        logs.push(['down', { foo: foo_val_teardown, bar: bar_val_teardown }]);
+    };
+});
+
+console.log('\n1. Initial run:');
+flushSync();
+
+console.log('\n2. Change foo from 0 to 1:');
+set(foo, 1);
+flushSync();
+
+console.log('\n3. Results:');
+logs.forEach((log, i) => {
+    console.log(`  ${i}:`, JSON.stringify(log));
+});
+
+// Check the teardown log
+const down_log = logs.find(log => log[0] === 'down');
+if (down_log) {
+    console.log('\nTeardown log found:', JSON.stringify(down_log[1]));
+    if (down_log[1].foo === 0 && down_log[1].bar === 0) {
+        console.log('✓ TEST PASSED: Both foo and bar show OLD values in teardown');
+    } else if (down_log[1].foo === 0 && down_log[1].bar === 2) {
+        console.log('✗ TEST FAILED: foo shows old value (0) but bar shows NEW value (2) instead of old value (0)');
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ TEST FAILED: Unexpected values in teardown');
+    }
+} else {
+    console.log('\n✗ TEST FAILED: No teardown log found');
+}

+// Edge case tests
+
+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { source, set } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import { derived } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+import { effect } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { prop } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js';
+import { get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';
+import { PROPS_IS_UPDATED, PROPS_IS_RUNES } from './packages/svelte/src/constants.js';
+
+console.log('\n=== Edge Case Tests ===\n');
+
+// Test 1: Derived that evaluates to null
+console.log('Test 1: Derived that evaluates to null');
+{
+    let logs = [];
+    const foo = source(null);
+    const bar = derived(() => get(foo));
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const val = get(bar);
+        logs.push(['up', val]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            logs.push(['down', get(bar)]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    set(foo, 'hello');
+    flushSync();
+    
+    if (logs[1][0] === 'down' && logs[1][1] === null) {
+        console.log('✓ Derived returning null works correctly');
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ Failed:', JSON.stringify(logs));
+    }
+}
+
+// Test 2: Derived with no dependencies
+console.log('\nTest 2: Derived with no dependencies (constant)');
+{
+    let logs = [];
+    const bar = derived(() => 42);
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const val = get(bar);
+        logs.push(['up', val]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            logs.push(['down', get(bar)]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    
+    if (logs[0][0] === 'up' && logs[0][1] === 42) {
+        console.log('✓ Constant derived works correctly');
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ Failed:', JSON.stringify(logs));
+    }
+}
+
+// Test 3: Prop that is undefined
+console.log('\nTest 3: Prop with undefined value');
+{
+    const parent_props = { optional: undefined };
+    const optional_prop = prop(parent_props, 'optional', PROPS_IS_RUNES | PROPS_IS_UPDATED, null);
+    
+    let ondestroy_value = 'not set';
+    let deps = source(0);
+

+        get(deps);

+    flushSync();

+        console.log('✓ Prop with undefined value works correctly, got:', ondestroy_value);
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ Failed: ondestroy_value =', ondestroy_value);
+    }
+}

+// Test 4: Multiple teardowns in sequence
+console.log('\nTest 4: Multiple teardowns in sequence');
+{
+    let logs = [];
+    const foo = source(0);
+    const bar = derived(() => get(foo) * 2);
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const val = get(bar);
+        logs.push(['up', val]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            logs.push(['down', get(bar)]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    
+    for (let i = 1; i <= 3; i++) {
+        set(foo, i);
+        flushSync();
+    }
+

+    const expected = [
+        ['up', 0],
+        ['down', 0], ['up', 2],

+        ['down', 4], ['up', 6]
+    ];
+    
+    let passed = true;
+    for (let i = 0; i < expected.length; i++) {
+        if (JSON.stringify(logs[i]) !== JSON.stringify(expected[i])) {
+            passed = false;
+            break;
+        }
+    }
+    
+    if (passed) {
+        console.log('✓ Multiple teardowns work correctly');
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ Failed:');
+        console.log('  Expected:', JSON.stringify(expected));
+        console.log('  Got:     ', JSON.stringify(logs));
+    }
+}
+
+console.log('\n=== All edge case tests completed ===\n');

+// Test script to reproduce the issue described in the PR
+// This tests that derived values return the old value when read during effect teardown
+
+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { source, set } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import { derived } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+import { effect } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';
+
+// Test 1: Verify that $state returns old value in teardown
+console.log('\n=== Test 1: $state in effect teardown ===');
+let state_logs = [];
+{
+    const foo = source(false);
+    const bar = source(false);
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const foo_val = get(foo);
+        const bar_val = get(bar);
+        state_logs.push(['up', { foo: foo_val, bar: bar_val }]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            const foo_val_teardown = get(foo);
+            const bar_val_teardown = get(bar);
+            state_logs.push(['down', { foo: foo_val_teardown, bar: bar_val_teardown }]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    console.log('After first effect run:', JSON.stringify(state_logs));
+    
+    set(foo, true);
+    set(bar, true);
+    flushSync();
+    console.log('After state change:', JSON.stringify(state_logs));
+    
+    // Expected: down log should show { foo: false, bar: false }
+    const down_log = state_logs[1];
+    if (down_log[0] === 'down' && down_log[1].foo === false && down_log[1].bar === false) {
+        console.log('✓ Test 1 PASSED: $state returns old value in teardown');
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ Test 1 FAILED: Expected { foo: false, bar: false }, got', JSON.stringify(down_log[1]));
+    }
+}
+
+// Test 2: Verify that $derived returns old value in teardown
+console.log('\n=== Test 2: $derived in effect teardown ===');
+let derived_logs = [];
+{
+    const foo = source(false);
+    const bar = derived(() => get(foo));
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const foo_val = get(foo);
+        const bar_val = get(bar);
+        derived_logs.push(['up', { foo: foo_val, bar: bar_val }]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            const foo_val_teardown = get(foo);
+            const bar_val_teardown = get(bar);
+            derived_logs.push(['down', { foo: foo_val_teardown, bar: bar_val_teardown }]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    console.log('After first effect run:', JSON.stringify(derived_logs));
+    
+    set(foo, true);
+    flushSync();
+    console.log('After state change:', JSON.stringify(derived_logs));
+    
+    // Expected: down log should show { foo: false, bar: false }
+    const down_log = derived_logs[1];
+    if (down_log[0] === 'down' && down_log[1].foo === false && down_log[1].bar === false) {
+        console.log('✓ Test 2 PASSED: $derived returns old value in teardown');
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ Test 2 FAILED: Expected { foo: false, bar: false }, got', JSON.stringify(down_log[1]));
+    }
+}
+
+console.log('\n=== Done ===');

+// Test the exact scenarios from the PR description
+
+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { source, set } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import { derived } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/deriveds.js';
+import { effect, component_root } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { prop } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js';
+import { get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';
+import { PROPS_IS_UPDATED, PROPS_IS_RUNES, PROPS_IS_BINDABLE } from './packages/svelte/src/constants.js';
+
+console.log('\n=== Testing PR Scenarios ===\n');
+
+// Scenario 1: From first PR - $derived in $effect teardown
+console.log('Scenario 1: $derived should show previous value in $effect teardown');
+{
+    let foo = source(false);
+    let bar = derived(() => get(foo));
+    let logs = [];
+    
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const foo_val = get(foo);
+        const bar_val = get(bar);
+        logs.push(['up', { foo: foo_val, bar: bar_val }]);
+        
+        return () => {
+            const foo_val = get(foo);
+            const bar_val = get(bar);
+            logs.push(['down', { foo: foo_val, bar: bar_val }]);
+        };
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    set(foo, true);
+    flushSync();
+    
+    // Expected: down should show { foo: false, bar: false }
+    const down_log = logs[1];
+    if (down_log && down_log[0] === 'down' && down_log[1].foo === false && down_log[1].bar === false) {
+        console.log('✓ PASSED: $derived returns old value in teardown');
+        console.log('  Expected: { foo: false, bar: false }');
+        console.log('  Got:      ', JSON.stringify(down_log[1]));
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ FAILED: $derived does not return old value');
+        console.log('  Expected: { foo: false, bar: false }');
+        console.log('  Got:      ', JSON.stringify(down_log ? down_log[1] : 'no log'));
+    }
+}
+
+// Scenario 2: From second PR - prop with setter but no getter in onDestroy
+console.log('\nScenario 2: Prop with setter but no getter should not be null in onDestroy');
+{
+    // Simulate the component scenario
+    let count = source(0);
+    let checked_in_ondestroy = null;
+    
+    function Child(checked_value) {
+        const props = { checked: checked_value };
+        
+        // Create prop with setter (has PROPS_IS_UPDATED flag)
+        // Simulate: let { checked } = $props();
+        const checked = prop(props, 'checked', PROPS_IS_RUNES | PROPS_IS_UPDATED, false);
+        
+        return component_root(() => {
+            // Simulate: <button onclick={() => checked = !checked}>
+            // This means checked has a setter
+            
+            // Simulate onDestroy
+            effect(() => {
+                return () => {
+                    // In real code, this would be onDestroy(() => { ... })
+                    checked_in_ondestroy = checked();
+                };
+            });
+        });
+    }
+    
+    // Mount component with checked=true
+    let child_root = null;
+    const eff = effect(() => {
+        const count_val = get(count);
+        
+        if (count_val === 0) {
+            // Mount
+            child_root = Child(true);
+        } else {
+            // Unmount
+            if (child_root) {
+                child_root();
+                child_root = null;
+            }
+        }
+    });
+    
+    flushSync();
+    
+    // Trigger unmount
+    set(count, 1);
+    flushSync();
+    
+    if (checked_in_ondestroy !== null) {
+        console.log('✓ PASSED: Prop value is not null in onDestroy');
+        console.log('  Expected: not null');
+        console.log('  Got:      ', checked_in_ondestroy);
+    } else {
+        console.log('✗ FAILED: Prop value is null in onDestroy');
+        console.log('  Expected: not null');
+        console.log('  Got:      ', checked_in_ondestroy);
+    }
+}
+
+console.log('\n=== PR Scenario Tests Complete ===\n');

+set(deps_in_effect, 1);

+

+// This is similar to: let { checked = false } = $props(); <button onclick={() => checked = !checked}>

+    };

+console.log('Expected: false or true, Got:', ondestroy_value);

+// Debug scenario 2
+
+import { flushSync } from './packages/svelte/src/index-client.js';
+import { source, set } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/sources.js';
+import { effect, component_root } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/effects.js';
+import { prop } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/reactivity/props.js';
+import { get } from './packages/svelte/src/internal/client/runtime.js';

+console.log('\n=== Debug Scenario 2 ===\n');
+
+let count = source(0);
+let checked_in_ondestroy = null;
+
+function Child(checked_value) {
+    const props = { checked: checked_value };
+    console.log('  Child created with props.checked =', checked_value);
+    
+    // Create prop with setter (has PROPS_IS_UPDATED flag)
+    const checked = prop(props, 'checked', PROPS_IS_RUNES | PROPS_IS_UPDATED, false);
+    console.log('  Prop created');
+    
+    return component_root(() => {
+        console.log('  Component root running');
+        
+        // The key issue: prop has setter but we never call it
+        // In the real scenario, there would be: <button onclick={() => checked = !checked}>
+        // But we DON'T read it in the template: no {checked}
+        
+        // onDestroy
+        effect(() => {
+            console.log('  Effect running');
+            return () => {
+                console.log('  onDestroy running');
+                checked_in_ondestroy = checked();
+                console.log('  Read checked in onDestroy:', checked_in_ondestroy);
+            };
+        });
+    });
+}

+let child_root = null;
+const eff = effect(() => {
+    const count_val = get(count);
+    console.log('Parent effect, count =', count_val);
+    
+    if (count_val === 0) {
+        // Mount
+        console.log('Mounting child...');
+        child_root = Child(true);
+    } else {
+        // Unmount
+        console.log('Unmounting child...');
+        if (child_root) {
+            child_root();
+            child_root = null;
+        }
+    }
+});
+
+flushSync();
+console.log('\nAfter mount, checked_in_ondestroy =', checked_in_ondestroy);
+
+// Trigger unmount
+console.log('\nTriggering unmount...');
+set(count, 1);
+flushSync();
+
+console.log('\nAfter unmount, checked_in_ondestroy =', checked_in_ondestroy);
